 kanchan chandara ke anusaar bijepi ke 15 pratishat saansad parivaravaadi hai
 Including all parties in the current Lok Sabha, 22 percent of mps are family members
 22 pratishat matlab 100 se adhik saansad
 24 percent of ministers in Modi's government are associated with familyism
 tippaniyan Mayawati said that while promoting Swami Prasad Maurya in twentyap, he was promoting his family
 ab bispi ne bhi parivaarwaad kaa khub paalan kiya he
 Our colleague Ravish Ranjan Shukla has done a quick research in UP
 isse pataa lagata he ki kai ilaake pariwaron kii chapet main he
 These families interfere in more than one party
 baharich main shah parivaar kaa siyaasi dabadabaa he
 The ailing Waqar Ahmed Shah is an MLA from Bahraich city, has been the Labor Minister in the SP government
 inaki patni ruwab saidaa baharich se saansad rahi
 His son Yasir Shah is Transport, Power Minister in SP government
 balram yadav sapa sarkaar main mantri rahe, saansad bhi rahe hai
 Son Sangram Yadav is an MLA from Atraulia
 basapa ke netaa or purv mantri nasimuddin siddiki banda se vidhaan parshad hai
 His son Afzal Siddiqui is also a ticket holder
 khud rajakishor singh sapa ke haraiya se vidhayak or mantri rahe hai
 His brother Dimple Singh is the SP candidate from Rudauli
 gonda ke kuvanr khandaan kii kahani par to serial ban saktaa he
 Kunwar Anand Singh, SP MLA from Gaura, is a cabinet minister
 is baar ve sapa se apni jagah naati ke liye tikat maang rahe hai
 But his son Kirtivardhan Singh is an MP from BJP
 saansad kirtivardhan singh ke chachere bhai vikram singh sapa se tikat maang rahe hai
 They may have to fight independantly due to Shivpal group
 gonda ke hi pandit singh jo sapa ke gonda sadar se vidhayak hai or krishi cabinet mantri he
 She herself is seeking tickets from Surajganj and is seeking tickets for son Suraj from Gonda Sadar
 ajay pratap singh urf lallaa bhayya congress se karnel ganj se vidhayak rah chuke hai
 His sister Brij Kunwari has been an MLA from BSP to Karnail Ganj
 ab lallaa bhayya bijepi jwine karke apana yaa apane bete ke naam se tikat maang rahe hai
 This family interferes with three parties
 mujffarnagar se bispi se saansad rahe hai kaadir rana
 His wife Saeeda Begum got a ticket from BSP for Budhana
 bhai nur saleem rana charathaval se bispi se hi tikat mila he

 By the way, it seems that looking at this list, the issue of familyism should be declared a end in politics
 hamane kai sahyogiyon se poocha sabane yahi kaha ki kisi ko is baat se fark nahin padataa ki parivaarwaad se raajnneeti ko nuksaan hota he

 congress ke 44 saansadon main kareeb 21 saansad parivaravaadi prishthbhumi se hai

 'aaj Tak' Hindi debate competition was organized at the famous Vasant Valley School in Delhi
 do din kii is vaad-vivaad pratiyogita kaa shuukravaar ko final round tha
 The theme was- Fairness is more important to the media than nationalism
 kaarykram main schuli chaatro ne bebaaki se apni raay rakhi

 pratiyogia main 27 skulon ne liya hissaa'aaj tak hindi vaad vivaad pratiyogita' ke final round kaa vishay jitna gambhir tha chaatro ke liye tark pesh karne kii chunauti bhi utani zyada
 27 schools of delhi-ncr participated in this competition organized in three phases
 pehle charan main oxford style dibet, duusare charan main turn kot or tisare charan main sansadeey vaad-vivaad pratiyogita kaa aayojan hua
 Gyan Bharti School and DPS RK Puram School reached the final round, performing brilliantly in the first two stages

 kya he is seat kaa itihaas
 
 
 Before delimitation, Dindori Lok Sabha seat used to be part of Malegaon
 us vakt yah janata dal kaa garh bhi kaha jaataa tha
 Yadav Narayan Jadhav of Praja Samajwadi Party became MP in 1957
 phir 1962 main congress satta main ai
 Madhav Laxman Jadhav reached Lok Sabha
 1967 or 1971 main jhamaru mangalu khhandol congress kii tikat se saansad bane
 Then in 1977 Haribhau Mahale won the election of MP from Bharatiya Lok Dal ticket
 lekin 1980 main jhamaru mangalu khhandole ne congress ko ek baar phir jeet dilaai
 In 1984, Sitaram Bhoye of Congress won, and in 1989 Haribhau Mahale made a comeback to the Janata Dal
 1991 main phir khhandole saansad bane
 In 1996, Kachru Bhau Rout got bjp's entry on this seat
 lekin 1998 main jhamaru mangalu khhandole jite
 In 1999, Haribhau Mahale succeeded in winning the Janata Dal (S)
 haalanki, 2004 main harishchandra chavaan jite
 After this, after the Dindori Lok Sabha seat came into existence, in 2009 and 2014, he again managed to win from here

 Know what is a surgical strike
 
 
 1
 In any limited area, when the army takes military action to damage and kill enemies and terrorists, it is called a surgical strike
 2
 In surgical strikes, it is kept in mind that only the place or area where terrorists or enemies are hidden should be targeted and it does not harm any other people
 3
 Actually, wherever surgical strikes are done, concrete information is collected first
 uske baad samay tay kiya jaataa he ki sargical strike kab karnaa he
 Then the information about this campaign is kept very confidential, whose information is available only to a select few
 4
 To carry out this operation, the command of the Army Special Commando is assigned
 5
 12 night from India
 30 baje se 2
